# Data sources catalog (Hawaii, Virginia & Federal)

Generated from `logs/manifest.csv` (deduplicated by file path) plus `data/cleaned/` extracts.

Regenerate after new downloads: `python scripts/generate_docs.py`

## Collection overview

| Item | Location | Count |
| --- | --- | ---: |
| Hawaii state downloads | `data/raw/hawaii/` | 78 |
| Virginia state downloads | `data/raw/virginia/` | 220 |
| Federal national downloads | `data/raw/federal/` | 466 |
| — CRDC public-use zips | `data/raw/federal/crdc/` | 2 |
| — Ed-tech / internet surveys | `data/raw/federal/edtech/` | 55 |
| Hawaii cleaned extracts | `data/cleaned/hawaii/` | 50 |
| Virginia cleaned extracts | `data/cleaned/virginia/` | 50 |
| **Total cataloged files** | | **864** |

## Primary portals used

| Portal | Used for |
| --- | --- |
| [Hawaii DOE / hawaiipublicschools.org](https://hawaiipublicschools.org/) | Hawaii enrollment, reports, PDF catalog |
| [hcnp.hawaii.gov/fiscal](https://hcnp.hawaii.gov/fiscal/) | Hawaii child nutrition / fiscal reports |
| [Virginia Open Data (data.virginia.gov)](https://data.virginia.gov/) | Bulk Virginia VDOE datasets (CKAN API) |
| [NCES CCD](https://nces.ed.gov/ccd/) | National school directory (filtered to HI/VA) |
| [CRDC / civilrightsdata.ed.gov](https://civilrightsdata.ed.gov/) | CRDC public-use zips (2015-16, 2017-18, 2020-21) |
| [CRDC / data.ed.gov](https://data.ed.gov/) | Individual CRDC spreadsheets; HI/VA cleaned extracts |
| [NCES FRSS](https://nces.ed.gov/surveys/frss/) | Fast Response Survey System — technology in schools |

## Raw vs cleaned

- **`data/raw/`** — original files downloaded from state or federal websites.
- **`data/cleaned/`** — Hawaii- or Virginia-only rows extracted from federal NCES and CRDC national files (not copies of the raw state downloads).
